liquid handling robots, plate readers, pumps, scales, heater shakers, and other lab automation equipment. Read \u003ca href=\"https://www.cell.com/device/fulltext/S2666-9986(23)00170-9\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003ethe paper\u003c/a\u003e in Device.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAdvantages over proprietary software:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCross-platform\u003c/strong\u003e: PyLabRobot works on Windows, macOS, and Linux. Many other interfaces are Windows-only.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eUniversal\u003c/strong\u003e: PyLabRobot works with any supported liquid handling robot, plate reader, pump, scale, heater shaker, etc. through a single interface.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFast iteration\u003c/strong\u003e: PyLabRobot enables rapid development of protocols using atomic commands run interactively in Jupyter notebooks or the Python REPL. This decreases iteration time from minutes to seconds.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eOpen-source\u003c/strong\u003e: PyLabRobot is open-source and free to use.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eControl\u003c/strong\u003e: With Python, you have ultimate flexibility to control your lab automation equipment. style=\"text-align: center\" align=\"center\"\u003e","\u003cimg width=\"400\" src=\".github/img/logo.png\" /\u003e","\u003c/div\u003e","","\u003cdiv style=\"text-align: center\" align=\"center\"\u003e","\u003ca href=\"https://docs.pylabrobot.org\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eDocs\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/a\u003e |","\u003ca href=\"https://discuss.pylabrobot.org\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eForum\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/a\u003e |","\u003ca href=\"https://docs.pylabrobot.org/user_guide/_getting-started/installation.html\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eInstallation\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/a\u003e |","\u003ca href=\"https://docs.pylabrobot.org/basic.html\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eGetting started\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/a\u003e","\u003c/div\u003e","","## What is PyLabRobot?","","PyLabRobot is a hardware agnostic, pure Python library for liquid handling robots, plate readers, pumps, scales, heater shakers, and other lab automation equipment. Read [the paper](\u003chttps://www.cell.com/device/fulltext/S2666-9986(23)00170-9\u003e) in Device.","","Advantages over proprietary software:","","- **Cross-platform**: PyLabRobot works on Windows, macOS, and Linux. Many other interfaces are Windows-only.","- **Universal**: PyLabRobot works with any supported liquid handling robot, plate reader, pump, scale, heater shaker, etc. through a single interface.","- **Fast iteration**: PyLabRobot enables rapid development of protocols using atomic commands run interactively in Jupyter notebooks or the Python REPL. This decreases iteration time from minutes to seconds.","- **Open-source**: PyLabRobot is open-source and free to use.","- **Control**: With Python, you have ultimate flexibility to control your lab automation equipment. You can write Turing-complete protocols that include feedback loops.","- **Modern**: PyLabRobot is built on modern Python 3.9+ features and async/await syntax.","- **Fast support**: PyLabRobot has [an active community forum](https://discuss.pylabrobot.org) for support and discussion, and most pull requests are merged within a day.","","### Liquid handling robots ([docs](https://docs.pylabrobot.org/user_guide/00_liquid-handling/_liquid-handling.html))","","PyLabRobot enables the use of any liquid handling robot through a single universal interface, that works on any modern operating system (Windows, macOS, Linux). We currently support Hamilton STAR, Hamilton Vantage, Tecan Freedom EVO, and Opentrons OT-2 robots, but we will soon support many more.","","Here's a quick example showing how to move 100uL of liquid from well A1 to A2 using firmware on **Hamilton STAR** (this will work on any operating system!):","","```python","from pylabrobot.liquid_handling import LiquidHandler","from pylabrobot.liquid_handling.backends import STARBackend","from pylabrobot.resources import Deck","","deck = Deck.load_from_json_file(\"hamilton-layout.json\")","lh = LiquidHandler(backend=STARBackend(), deck=deck)","await lh.setup()","","await lh.pick_up_tips(lh.deck.get_resource(\"tip_rack\")[\"A1\"])","await lh.aspirate(lh.deck.get_resource(\"plate\")[\"A1\"], vols=100)","await lh.dispense(lh.deck.get_resource(\"plate\")[\"A2\"], vols=100)","await lh.return_tips()","```","","To run the same protocol on an **Opentrons**, use the following:","","```python","from pylabrobot.liquid_handling.backends import OpentronsOT2Backend","deck = Deck.load_from_json_file(\"opentrons-layout.json\")","lh = LiquidHandler(backend=OpentronsOT2Backend(host=\"x.x.x.x\"), deck=deck)","```","","Or **Tecan** (also works on any operating system!):","","```python","from pylabrobot.liquid_handling.backends import EVOBackend","deck = Deck.load_from_json_file(\"tecan-layout.json\")","lh = LiquidHandler(backend=EVOBackend(), deck=deck)","```","","We also provide a browser-based Visualizer which can visualize the state of the deck during a run, and can be used to develop and test protocols without a physical robot.","","![Visualizer](.github/img/visualizer.png)","","### Plate readers ([docs](https://docs.pylabrobot.org/user_guide/02_analytical/plate-reading/plate-reading.html))","","Moving a plate to a ClarioStar using a liquid handler, and reading luminescence:","","```python","from pylabrobot.plate_reading import PlateReader, CLARIOstarBackend","","pr = PlateReader(name=\"plate reader\", backend=CLARIOstarBackend(), size_x=1, size_y=1, size_z=1)","await pr.setup()","","# Use in combination with a liquid handler","lh.assign_child_resource(pr, location=Coordinate(x, y, z))","lh.move_plate(lh.deck.get_resource(\"plate\"), pr)","","data = await pr.read_luminescence()","```","","For Cytation5, use the `Cytation5` backend.","","### Centrifuges ([docs](https://docs.pylabrobot.org/user_guide/01_material-handling/centrifuge/_centrifuge.html))","","Centrifugation at 800g for 60 seconds:","","```python","from pylabrobot.centrifuge import Centrifuge, VSpin","cf = Centrifuge(backend=VSpin(bucket_1_position=0), name=\"centrifuge\", size_x=1, size_y=1, size_z=1)","await cf.setup()","","await cf.start_spin_cycle(g = 800, duration = 60)","```","","### Pumps ([docs](https://docs.pylabrobot.org/user_guide/00_liquid-handling/pumps/_pumps.html))","","Pumping at 100 rpm for 30 seconds using a Masterflex pump:","","```python","from pylabrobot.pumps import Pump","from pylabrobot.pumps.cole_parmer.masterflex import Masterflex","","p = Pump(backend=Masterflex())","await p.setup()","await p.run_for_duration(speed=100, duration=30)","```","","### Scales ([docs](https://docs.pylabrobot.org/user_guide/02_analytical/scales.html))","","Taking a measurement from a Mettler Toledo scale:","","```python","from pylabrobot.scales import Scale","from pylabrobot.scales.mettler_toledo import MettlerToledoWXS205SDU","","backend = MettlerToledoWXS205SDU(port=\"/dev/cu.usbserial-110\")","scale = Scale(backend=backend, size_x=0, size_y=0, size_z=0)","await scale.setup()","","weight = await scale.get_weight()","```","","### Heater shakers ([docs](https://docs.pylabrobot.org/user_guide/01_material-handling/heating-shaking.html))","","Setting the temperature of a heater shaker to 37\u0026deg;C:","","```python","from pylabrobot.heating_shaking import HeaterShaker, InhecoThermoShakeBackend","","backend = InhecoThermoShakeBackend()","hs = HeaterShaker(backend=backend, name=\"HeaterShaker\", size_x=0, size_y=0, size_z=0)","await hs.setup()","await hs.set_temperature(37)","```","","### Fans ([docs](https://docs.pylabrobot.org/user_guide/01_material-handling/fans/fans.html))","","Running a fan at 100% intensity for one minute:","","```python","from pylabrobot.only_fans import Fan","from pylabrobot.only_fans import HamiltonHepaFanBackend","","fan = Fan(backend=HamiltonHepaFanBackend(), name=\"my fan\")","await fan.setup()","await fan.turn_on(intensity=100, duration=60)","```","","### Thermocyclers ([docs](https://docs.pylabrobot.org/user_guide/01_material-handling/thermocycling/thermocycling.html))","","Running a thermocycler with a simple protocol:","","```python","await tc.run_pcr_profile(","  denaturation_temp=98.0,","  denaturation_time=10.0,","  annealing_temp=55.0,","  annealing_time=30.0,","  extension_temp=72.0,","  extension_time=60.0,","  num_cycles=2,","  block_max_volume=25.0,","  lid_temperature=105.0,","  pre_denaturation_temp=95.0,","  pre_denaturation_time=180.0,","  final_extension_temp=72.0,","  final_extension_time=300.0,","  storage_temp=4.0,","  storage_time=600.0,",")","```","","## Resources","","### Documentation","","[docs.pylabrobot.org](https://docs.pylabrobot.org)","","- [Installation](https://docs.pylabrobot.org/user_guide/_getting-started/installation.html)","- [Getting Started](https://docs.pylabrobot.org/user_guide/index.html)","- <div align="center" dir="auto">

<a href="https://discuss.pylabrobot.org" rel="nofollow"><strong>Forum</strong></a> |

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">What is PyLabRobot?</h2><a id="user-content-what-is-pylabrobot" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: What is PyLabRobot?" href="#what-is-pylabrobot"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">PyLabRobot is a hardware agnostic, pure Python library for liquid handling robots, plate readers, pumps, scales, heater shakers, and other lab automation equipment. Read <a href="https://www.cell.com/device/fulltext/S2666-9986(23)00170-9" rel="nofollow">the paper</a> in Device.</p>
<p dir="auto">Advantages over proprietary software:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Cross-platform</strong>: PyLabRobot works on Windows, macOS, and Linux. Many other interfaces are Windows-only.</li>
<li><strong>Universal</strong>: PyLabRobot works with any supported liquid handling robot, plate reader, pump, scale, heater shaker, etc. through a single interface.</li>
<li><strong>Fast iteration</strong>: PyLabRobot enables rapid development of protocols using atomic commands run interactively in Jupyter notebooks or the Python REPL. This decreases iteration time from minutes to seconds.</li>
<li><strong>Open-source</strong>: PyLabRobot is open-source and free to use.</li>
<li><strong>Control</strong>: With Python, you have ultimate flexibility to control your lab automation equipment. You can write Turing-complete protocols that include feedback loops.</li>
<li><strong>Modern</strong>: PyLabRobot is built on modern Python 3.9+ features and async/await syntax.</li>
<li><strong>Fast support</strong>: PyLabRobot has <a href="https://discuss.pylabrobot.org" rel="nofollow">an active community forum</a> for support and discussion, and most pull requests are merged within a day.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Liquid handling robots (<a href="https://docs.pylabrobot.org/user_guide/00_liquid-handling/_liquid-handling.html" rel="nofollow">docs</a>)</h3><a id="user-content-liquid-handling-robots-docs" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Liquid handling robots (docs)" href="#liquid-handling-robots-docs"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">PyLabRobot enables the use of any liquid handling robot through a single universal interface, that works on any modern operating system (Windows, macOS, Linux). We currently support Hamilton STAR, Hamilton Vantage, Tecan Freedom EVO, and Opentrons OT-2 robots, but we will soon support many more.</p>
<p dir="auto">Here's a quick example showing how to move 100uL of liquid from well A1 to A2 using firmware on <strong>Hamilton STAR</strong> (this will work on any operating system!):</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="from pylabrobot.liquid_handling import LiquidHandler
from pylabrobot.liquid_handling.backends import STARBackend
from pylabrobot.resources import Deck

deck = Deck.load_from_json_file(&quot;hamilton-layout.json&quot;)
lh = LiquidHandler(backend=STARBackend(), deck=deck)
await lh.setup()

await lh.pick_up_tips(lh.deck.get_resource(&quot;tip_rack&quot;)[&quot;A1&quot;])
await lh.aspirate(lh.deck.get_resource(&quot;plate&quot;)[&quot;A1&quot;], vols=100)
await lh.dispense(lh.deck.get_resource(&quot;plate&quot;)[&quot;A2&quot;], vols=100)
await lh.return_tips()"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">pylabrobot</span>.<span class="pl-s1">liquid_handling</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">LiquidHandler</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">pylabrobot</span>.<span class="pl-s1">liquid_handling</span>.<span class="pl-s1">backends</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">STARBackend</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">pylabrobot</span>.<span class="pl-s1">resources</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">Deck</span>

<span class="pl-s1">deck</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Deck</span>.<span class="pl-c1">load_from_json_file</span>(<span class="pl-s">"hamilton-layout.json"</span>)
<span class="pl-s1">lh</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">LiquidHandler</span>(<span class="pl-s1">backend</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-en">STARBackend</span>(), <span class="pl-s1">deck</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">deck</span>)
<span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">lh</span>.<span class="pl-c1">setup</span>()

<span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">lh</span>.<span class="pl-c1">pick_up_tips</span>(<span class="pl-s1">lh</span>.<span class="pl-c1">deck</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get_resource</span>(<span class="pl-s">"tip_rack"</span>)[<span class="pl-s">"A1"</span>])
<span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">lh</span>.<span class="pl-c1">aspirate</span>(<span class="pl-s1">lh</span>.<span class="pl-c1">deck</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get_resource</span>(<span class="pl-s">"plate"</span>)[<span class="pl-s">"A1"</span>], <span class="pl-s1">vols</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">100</span>)
<span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">lh</span>.<span class="pl-c1">dispense</span>(<span class="pl-s1">lh</span>.<span class="pl-c1">deck</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get_resource</span>(<span class="pl-s">"plate"</span>)[<span class="pl-s">"A2"</span>], <span class="pl-s1">vols</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">100</span>)
<span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">lh</span>.<span class="pl-c1">return_tips</span>()</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">To run the same protocol on an <strong>Opentrons</strong>, use the following:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="from pylabrobot.liquid_handling.backends import OpentronsOT2Backend
deck = Deck.load_from_json_file(&quot;opentrons-layout.json&quot;)
lh = LiquidHandler(backend=OpentronsOT2Backend(host=&quot;x.x.x.x&quot;), deck=deck)"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">pylabrobot</span>.<span class="pl-s1">liquid_handling</span>.<span class="pl-s1">backends</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">OpentronsOT2Backend</span>
<span class="pl-s1">deck</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Deck</span>.<span class="pl-c1">load_from_json_file</span>(<span class="pl-s">"opentrons-layout.json"</span>)
<span class="pl-s1">lh</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">LiquidHandler</span>(<span class="pl-s1">backend</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-en">OpentronsOT2Backend</span>(<span class="pl-s1">host</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"x.x.x.x"</span>), <span class="pl-s1">deck</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">deck</span>)</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Or <strong>Tecan</strong> (also works on any operating system!):</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="from pylabrobot.liquid_handling.backends import EVOBackend
deck = Deck.load_from_json_file(&quot;tecan-layout.json&quot;)
lh = LiquidHandler(backend=EVOBackend(), deck=deck)"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">pylabrobot</span>.<span class="pl-s1">liquid_handling</span>.<span class="pl-s1">backends</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">EVOBackend</span>
<span class="pl-s1">deck</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Deck</span>.<span class="pl-c1">load_from_json_file</span>(<span class="pl-s">"tecan-layout.json"</span>)
<span class="pl-s1">lh</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">LiquidHandler</span>(<span class="pl-s1">backend</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-en">EVOBackend</span>(), <span class="pl-s1">deck</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">deck</span>)</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">We also provide a browser-based Visualizer which can visualize the state of the deck during a run, and can be used to develop and test protocols without a physical robot.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/PyLabRobot/pylabrobot/blob/main/.github/img/visualizer.png"><img src="/PyLabRobot/pylabrobot/raw/main/.github/img/visualizer.png" alt="Visualizer" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Plate readers (<a href="https://docs.pylabrobot.org/user_guide/02_analytical/plate-reading/plate-reading.html" rel="nofollow">docs</a>)</h3><a id="user-content-plate-readers-docs" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Plate readers (docs)" href="#plate-readers-docs"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Moving a plate to a ClarioStar using a liquid handler, and reading luminescence:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="from pylabrobot.plate_reading import PlateReader, CLARIOstarBackend

pr = PlateReader(name=&quot;plate reader&quot;, backend=CLARIOstarBackend(), size_x=1, size_y=1, size_z=1)
await pr.setup()

# Use in combination with a liquid handler
lh.assign_child_resource(pr, location=Coordinate(x, y, z))
lh.move_plate(lh.deck.get_resource(&quot;plate&quot;), pr)

data = await pr.read_luminescence()"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">pylabrobot</span>.<span class="pl-s1">plate_reading</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">PlateReader</span>, <span class="pl-v">CLARIOstarBackend</span>

<span class="pl-s1">pr</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">PlateReader</span>(<span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"plate reader"</span>, <span class="pl-s1">backend</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-en">CLARIOstarBackend</span>(), <span class="pl-s1">size_x</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span>, <span class="pl-s1">size_y</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span>, <span class="pl-s1">size_z</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span>)
<span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">pr</span>.<span class="pl-c1">setup</span>()

<span class="pl-c"># Use in combination with a liquid handler</span>
<span class="pl-s1">lh</span>.<span class="pl-c1">assign_child_resource</span>(<span class="pl-s1">pr</span>, <span class="pl-s1">location</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-en">Coordinate</span>(<span class="pl-s1">x</span>, <span class="pl-s1">y</span>, <span class="pl-s1">z</span>))
<span class="pl-s1">lh</span>.<span class="pl-c1">move_plate</span>(<span class="pl-s1">lh</span>.<span class="pl-c1">deck</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get_resource</span>(<span class="pl-s">"plate"</span>), <span class="pl-s1">pr</span>)

<span class="pl-s1">data</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">pr</span>.<span class="pl-c1">read_luminescence</span>()</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">For Cytation5, use the <code>Cytation5</code> backend.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Centrifuges (<a href="https://docs.pylabrobot.org/user_guide/01_material-handling/centrifuge/_centrifuge.html" rel="nofollow">docs</a>)</h3><a id="user-content-centrifuges-docs" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Centrifuges (docs)" href="#centrifuges-docs"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Resources</h2><a id="user-content-resources" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Resources" href="#resources"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
